# Report for classes

### New Class : [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230)

 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) **SubClassOf** [forelimb bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0005417)
 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) *[created by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by)* WD
 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) *[label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label)* forelimb wing bud
 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) **EquivalentTo** [forelimb bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0005417) **and** [has potential to develop into](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002387) **some** [forelimb wing](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000024)
 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) **SubClassOf** [has potential to develop into](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002387) **some** [forelimb wing](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000024)
 * [forelimb wing bud](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300230) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* A wing bud that develops into a wing

It is typically an elongate scale.[Mattox and Toledo-Piza 2012] { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=[https://doi.org/10.1111/j.1096-3642.2012.00830.x](https://doi.org/10.1111/j.1096-3642.2012.00830.x) }

### New Class : [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223)

 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) **EquivalentTo** [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224) **and** [composed primarily of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002473) **some** [bone tissue](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002481)
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) *[created by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by)* WD
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) **SubClassOf** [vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002412)
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) *[database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)* ZFA:0000263
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) *[database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)* TAO:0000263
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* Vertebral bone lacking hemal spines (Weitzman, 1962), refers generally to the anterior vertebral region bounding the abdominal cavity. Alternate but not quite synonymous terms are abdominal or trunk vertebrae, which bear parapophyses and ribs. In many actinopterygians dorsal to the posterior abdominal cavity there are transitional vertebrae lacking ribs but also without hemal spines or sometimes even enclosed hemal arches. The primary definition would identify these vertebrae as precaudal. Bird and Mabee, 2003. { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=[https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387](https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387) } 
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) *[label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label)* precaudal vertebra
 * [precaudal vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300223) **SubClassOf** [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224)

### New Class : [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224)

 * [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224) *[label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label)* precaudal vertebra endochondral element
 * [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* Vertebral elements lacking hemal spines (Weitzman, 1962), refers generally to the anterior vertebral region bounding the abdominal cavity. Alternate but not quite synonymous terms are abdominal or trunk vertebrae, which bear parapophyses and ribs. In many actinopterygians dorsal to the posterior abdominal cavity there are transitional vertebrae lacking ribs but also without hemal spines or sometimes even enclosed hemal arches. The primary definition would identify these vertebrae as precaudal.(Bird and Mabee, 2003) { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=[https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387](https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387) } 
 * [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224) **SubClassOf** [vertebral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0010913)

### New Class : [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225)

 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) **SubClassOf** [vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011094)
 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) *[label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label)* precaudal vertebra cartilage element
 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) **EquivalentTo** [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224) **and** [composed primarily of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002473) **some** [cartilage tissue](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002418)
 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* Vertebral cartilage elements lacking hemal spines (Weitzman, 1962), refers generally to the anterior vertebral region bounding the abdominal cavity. Alternate but not quite synonymous terms are abdominal or trunk vertebrae, which bear parapophyses and ribs. In many actinopterygians dorsal to the posterior abdominal cavity there are transitional vertebrae lacking ribs but also without hemal spines or sometimes even enclosed hemal arches. The primary definition would identify these vertebrae as precaudal.(Bird and Mabee, 2003) { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=[https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387](https://doi.org/10.1002/dvdy.10387) } 
 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) **SubClassOf** [precaudal vertebra endochondral element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300224)
 * [precaudal vertebra cartilage element](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/ext.owl/UBERON_4300225) *[created by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by)* WD

### Changes for: [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677)

 * _Deleted_
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)* TAO:0000263
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)* ZFA:0000263
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[external definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBPROP_0000001)* Post-Weberian vertebrae lacking hemal spines (Weitzman, 1962), refers generally to the anterior vertebral region bounding the abdominal cavity. Alternate but not quite synonymous terms are abdominal or trunk vertebrae, which bear parapophyses and ribs. In many actinopterygians dorsal to the posterior abdominal cavity there are transitional vertebrae lacking ribs but also without hemal spines or sometimes even enclosed hemal arches. The primary definition would identify these vertebrae as precaudal. Bird and Mabee, 2003.[TAO] { [date retrieved](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#date_retrieved)=2012-08-14 , [external class](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#external_class)=TAO:0000263 , [ontology](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#ontology)=TAO , [source](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#source)=ZFIN:curator } 
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[external ontology notes](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBPROP_0000012)* in TAO this is defined as post-Weberian, this may not precisely align with the definition of being part of the trunk { [external ontology](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#external_ontology)=TAO } 
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[has related synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym)* abdominal vertebra { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=TAO:0000263 } 
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[has related synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym)* abdominal vertebrae { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=TAO:0000263 } 
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[has related synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym)* precaudal vertebra { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=TAO:0000263 } 
    *  **-** [trunk vertebra](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0011677) *[has related synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym)* precaudal vertebrae { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=TAO:0000263 , [has synonym type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType)=[plural term](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/uberon/core#PLURAL) }
